LoadingScreen/Help53=Flamespitters are fragile but deal a lot of damage. They also slow down while attacking, so position them wisely and let them rip.
LoadingScreen/Help54=Hunters deal bonus damage to light units and can jump up cliffs. They make ideal units to harass enemy worker lines.
LoadingScreen/Help55=Horned Magus are potent offensive and defensive spell casters. Do not neglect their ability to sway fights.
LoadingScreen/Help56=Unseen Beasts cloak in the presence of enemy units. They can deal massive amounts of damage if not detected.
LoadingScreen/Help57=Berserkers are very tough for their cost. Use them to absorb damage for less durable Dragon units.
LoadingScreen/Help58=Skyrazers are deadly against flying units, but are otherwise unimpressive against land based targets.
LoadingScreen/Help59=Hands of Power are detectors and powerful casters. Their abilities can restrict enemy mobility and increase your own.
LoadingScreen/Help60=Brimstone Demolishers are engines of destruction. Do not neglect to upgrade Dragon Fire Attacks, which greatly improve their damage output.
LoadingScreen/Help61=Fleshrenders are the most mobile air unit, their ability to make lightning quick attacks can provide great map control.
LoadingScreen/Help62=Aurora Conduits can reduce enemy armor. Use them in combination with fast attacking units to deal massive amounts of damage.
LoadingScreen/Help63=Arkwyrms can unload units at a distance, allowing you to siege enemy base beyond the range of ground based anti-air.
LoadingScreen/Help64=Volcanic Harbingers deal increased damage and gain an area of effect attack with Overload. Allow them to charge up between shots to maximize their potential.
LoadingScreen/Help65=Grim Gliders are not just expensive detectors. They can raise the dead as weaker temporary Shades with Mortality's Eclipse, adding the slain on both sides to your own army.
LoadingScreen/Help66=Sunken Guardians temporary immobilze enemies when they strike them. They also benefit from Dragon Melee Attacks.
LoadingScreen/Help67=Phlogiston Guardians are detectors. They also benefit from Dragon Fire Attacks.
LoadingScreen/Help68=Dragon buildings benefit from Dragon Plate Armor. Their durability can be further increased with Dragon Lineage.
LoadingScreen/Help69=Dragon Fire Attacks increase the damage of all Dragon units and structures that attack with flame projectiles.
LoadingScreen/Help70=Dragon Melee Attacks increase the damage of all Dragon units and structures that attack with a physical extension of themselves.
LoadingScreen/Help71=Dragon Scale Armor increases the armor of all Light Dragon units.
LoadingScreen/Help72=Dragon Plate Armor increases the armor of all Armored Dragon units and structures.
LoadingScreen/Help73=Killing a primary Dragon structure destroys all of its propogated secondary structures.
LoadingScreen/Help74=Denizens of the Deep can convert between minerals and vespene gas when Abundance is upgraded.
LoadingScreen/Help75=Razorbacks have upgrades that can cause them to damage attackers, increase the amount of supply they provide, and make them more durable.
LoadingScreen/Help76=Fervid Reconstitution makes Flamespitters move faster when attacking instead of slower, as well as increasing their damage by 1. It is a must have to bring your Flamespitters on the offensive.
LoadingScreen/Help77=Feast increases maximum Hunter life and provides them with life gain on hit. It can elevate Hunters from harassment units to your core army.
LoadingScreen/Help78=The Horned Magus's Fire Shield can be used offensively or defensively. It increases the targets armor but it also deals great damage to all nearby units that aren't also fireshielded, enemy and ally alike.
LoadingScreen/Help79=The Horned Magus's Shroud can be used to get the jump on your enemies or to make a hasty get away.
LoadingScreen/Help80=The Horned Magus's Invigorate is one of the only way Dragon units can heal.
LoadingScreen/Help81=To build Unseen Beasts you must first research them in the Lesser Deep One's Augmentation Pit.
LoadingScreen/Help82=Unseen Beasts make excellent scouts in addition to crushing enemy worker lines with their Keep Senses ability and their high survivability.
LoadingScreen/Help83=Madness forces nearby enemies to attack Berserkers, preventing them from attacking your less durable units or escaping. It also makes them highly effective against Banelings.
LoadingScreen/Help84=Ember Core increases a Skyrazer's range by its current cliff level. This can increase its range by up to 3, making it an excellent defense against flying siege units.
LoadingScreen/Help85=The Hand of Power's Crushing Gravity also affects units that enter its area after it has been casted. It is extra effective against air units because it prevents them from attacking and forces them to the ground.
LoadingScreen/Help86=The Hand of Power's Frenzy affects all biological units. It can be used not only to increase the damage output of your units, but also to soften and clean up fleeing biological enemies.
LoadingScreen/Help87=Infernal Breath increases the range of Brimstone Demolishers, vastly increasing the amount of enemies they can roast.
LoadingScreen/Help88=Proliferation reduces the build time of Fleshrenders. This can be used to quickly build a large amount of map control, or to counter heavily specialized armies.
LoadingScreen/Help89=Celerity increases the rate at which Aurora Conduits attack, causing them not only to deal more damage but also further reduce enemy armor.
LoadingScreen/Help90=Plasma Catalyst increases the rate at which Volcanic Harbingers can produce Overload charges, allowing them to obliterate enemies more quickly than before.
LoadingScreen/Help91=Volcanic Harbingers deal splash damage to your own units with Overload. However, they never deal splash damage to Shades.
LoadingScreen/Help92=Wraith Night prevents Shades from decaying when near a friendly Grim Glider. This can cause a powerful push to be game ending.
LoadingScreen/Help93=Shades can't be controlled and deal half the damage and have half the life of their parent unit. This means that as your enemy accumulate upgrades, your Shades produced by their units are effectively weaker.
LoadingScreen/Help94=Dragon units with Fire attacks have Retarget, which prevents them from wasting shots.
LoadingScreen/Help95=Many Dragon units have different weapons for melee and ranged attacks which benefit from separate upgrades. Flamespitters for example deal reduced damage in melee.
LoadingScreen/Help96=Frontier Deep Ones have a more powerful version of Invigorate that can simultaneously heal large numbers of biological units.
LoadingScreen/Help97=Propogate Genesis Pits from your Deep Ones to increase your army production rate.
LoadingScreen/Help98=Propogate Augmentation Pits from your Deep Ones to access upgrades and higher tier units.
LoadingScreen/Help99=Dragon Lineage provides all Dragon units and structures with life regeneration outside of combat, as well as increasing the durability of Dragon structures.

Param/Value/lib_03673618_ABCE777C=In case you know nothing about this mod, here's the basics, i'll leave the rest for you to figure out yourself though.<n/><n/><c val="FFFF80">Basic Gameplay</c>:<n/><n/>- The Myco-Synaptic Choir, or MycoChoir for short, is your town hall, from it you can build every building the race has to offer at any time, anywhere on the map within a <c val="FF8000">Requisition Field</c>, much like in command and conquer, however, unlike in C&C the buildings with be built without interrupting the MycoChoir's function, so with a single one you can build any amount of structures simultaneously.  [Subject to change if necessary].<n/><n/>- The buildings on the second row are your productions structures, the <c val="FFFF80">Garrison</c>, the <c val="FFFF80">Assembly </c>and the <c val="FFFF80">Hangar</c>. Assigned to infantry, Mech and Air respectively, below them you have their specific tech structures you need to build next to progress further down the tech tree.<n/><n/>- The <c val="FF8000">Requisition Field</c> is the orange circle that surrounds the Myco-Processors and the (green circles around) Myco-Choirs and Greater Processors; its analogous to the protoss pylon energy field, however, it doesn't work in exactly the same manner. Some units and structures require the abilities to be cast within a requisition field, and all buildings, including some units, require a requisition field source nearby in order to function.<n/><n/>- All production buildings can be upgraded to a "super" variant that unlocks more advanced units and produces 25% faster, however, they require a <c val="80FF00">super requisition source (the green ones) </c>around them in order to function, in other words, a Myco-Choir and a Greater Processor nearby. You can upgrade Myco-Processors within super requisition sources into Greater Processors to expand the area. <n/><n/>- Prospectors [Name subject to change] are your main worker unit, they are used to build MycoChoirs, but can also transform into a number of defensive buildings that the MycoChoir is unable to deploy (for balance's sake).<n/><n/>- Servitors are your basic unit, they start off unable to attack air and only have slightly less health and DPS than a marine, however, they are smaller, cheaper, and can pack more of them in a smaller area, increasing their volume of fire. You can upgrade their health and equip them with missile launchers in the Bio-Synth Facility<n/><n/>- Cremators are an army defense unit, they have decent range and DPS and do damage in a line. While not nearly as mobile as hellions they can be upgraded to have a shield capable of intercepting missiles<n/><n/>- The Censer is your basic means of Bio healing, once their signature ability is enabled, they will become stationary and heal units in a decent radius, instead of bleeding energy, each heal will deplete energy, so be not afraid of using them.<n/><n/>- The warden airship is your basic means of transport, it can hold 2 extra units than the every other transport and it is capable of shielding and locking down enemy units at the cost of draining its own energy. - Hailstorm Turrets are your basic means of base defense, they can air and ground units, however they have separate weapons that work differently. The hellstorm missile pods are its basic readily available ground attack, which fires slow moving AOE projectiles that can be dodged by a unit that moves fast enough [Subject to change], <c val="FFFF80">The hailstorm dont start out with the anti-air weapon enabled, you have to enable it by researching it in the Satelite Uplink</c> [Subject to change]<n/><n/>- The Sat-Com Tower is a caster building useful for base defense, can reveal enemy units, repair mechanical units and summon small drones to help defend the base in case of emergencies. <n/><n/>- The Karolean Walker is your giant mech unit, slow but powerful long range attacks. Buffs friendly units by giving them +1 armor and +2 range directly under them, use them along the rest of your army for stronger pushes. Reveals iself while attacking.
